-- See the Meals!"/>         <meta itemprop="alternativeHeadline" content=""/>         <meta itemprop="image" content="https://media.zenfs.com/en_us/News/USWeekly/1416607913_michelle-obama-article.jpg"/>         <meta itemprop="description" content="Students tweets with the hashtag #ThanksMichelleObama have gone viral as they criticize their school cafeteria food -- see the nasty-looking meals here"/>         <p>Hangry! On Friday, Nov. 21, students started sarcastically tweeting <strong>#ThanksMichelleObama</strong> at the First Lady with photos of their not-so-tasty-looking cafeteria food.</p> <p><a href="http://www.usmagazine.com/celebrity-style/pictures/michelle-obamas-european-style-200919/35194?utm_source=yahoocelebrity&utm_medium=referral" target="_blank">PHOTOS:  Michelle&#39;s best style moments</a></p> <p>Michelle Obama, is, of course, behind the USDA&#39;s new guidelines for school lunches, and apparently the kids aren&#39;t into it.</p> <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" lang="en"> <p>Had a very #healthylunch today. The apple definitely made up for the &quot;mystery mush&quot; #ThanksMichelleObama pic.twitter.com/RWCnQRCxJK</p> — Hunter Whitney (@huntwhitney4) <a href="https://twitter.com/huntwhitney4/status/533039145216524288">November 13, 2014</a></blockquote> <p>   </p> <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" lang="en"> <p><a href="https://twitter.com/huntwhitney4">@huntwhitney4</a> looks like floor sweepings mixed into fructose</p> — Steve Etienne (@1Oyster1) <a href="https://twitter.com/1Oyster1/status/535553238943432705">November 20, 2014</a></blockquote> <p>   </p> <p><a href="http://www.usmagazine.com/celebrity-news/pictures/obama-family-album-20091812/5870?utm_source=yahoocelebrity&utm_medium=referral" target="_blank">PHOTOS: The Obama family album</a></p> <p>&quot;Had a very #healthylunch today. The apple definitely made up for the &#39;mystery mush&#39; #ThanksMichelleObama,&quot; one student tweeted along with a photo of an orange tray graced with only unappetizing &quot;mush&quot; and an apple.</p> <p>Another student replied to the likely still-hungry kid with: &quot;They call it spanish rice&quot; and &quot;@huntwhitney4 looks like floor sweepings mixed into fructose.&quot;</p> <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" lang="en"> <p>Yum school lunches #thanksmichelleobama pic.twitter.com/eS27j75Oae</p> — Jess Sency (@Jess_Sency) <a href="https://twitter.com/Jess_Sency/status/534735933682503683">November 18, 2014</a></blockquote> <p>   </p> <p><a href="http://www.usmagazine.com/celebrity-news/pictures/president-obamas-a-list-pals-201228/24150?utm_source=yahoocelebrity&utm_medium=referral" target="_blank">PHOTOS: Obama&#39;s A-list pals</a></p> <p>The meals are meant to be Thanksgiving related, but as another student argued, seem a far cry from patriotic turkey day trimmings. &quot;@Jess_Sency @Shutterbugfun What IS that supposed to be?&quot; one tweeted after a friend posted a picture of what was supposed to be baked beans.</p> <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" lang="en"> <p>my school lunch today #ThanksMichelleObama pic.twitter.com/2jeYlJF0wu</p> — josh russell (@josh_emerson) <a href="https://twitter.com/josh_emerson/status/535898049131069441">November 21, 2014</a></blockquote> <p>   </p> <p>The first lady has been adamant about her goal to end childhood obesity. In July, Barack Obama&#39;s wife said she&#39;d &quot;fight until the bitter end to make sure that every kid in this country continues to have the best nutrition that they can have.&quot;</p> <p><a href="http://www.usmagazine.com/celebrity-news/pictures/barack-obama-and-michelle-obamas-20th-wedding-anniversary-album-2012310/25317?utm_source=yahoocelebrity&utm_medium=referral" target="_blank">PHOTOS: Michelle and Obama&#39;s wedding album</a></p> <blockquote class="twitter-tweet" lang="en"> <p>Call this Mac and cheese? #thanksMichelleObama pic.twitter.com/ti3FBhCYeZ</p> — David?Suderback (@iWikeWice) <a href="https://twitter.com/iWikeWice/status/459376025982341121">April 24, 2014</a></blockquote> <p>   </p> <p>Under Obama&#39;s guidance, the USDA guidelines implemented limits on calories, fat, sugar, and sodium for all food and drinks sold during the school day for 100,000 schools across the country.</p> <ul id="topics" class="hidden"><li lunches</li></ul>         <!-- google_ad_section_end -->     </div> </div>  </section> <div id="mediacontentcomments" class="yom-mod yom-comments default ">     <a href="" class="pharma hidden">Click
